953  

954  

955class Device: 

956 """Represent a GPU and act as an entry point for cuda.core features. 

957  

958 This is a singleton object that helps ensure interoperability 

959 across multiple libraries imported in the process to both see 

960 and use the same GPU device. 

961  

962 While acting as the entry point, many other CUDA resources can be 

963 allocated such as streams and buffers. Any :obj:`~_context.Context` dependent 

964 resource created through this device, will continue to refer to 

965 this device's context. 

966  

967 Newly returned :obj:`~_device.Device` objects are thread-local singletons 

968 for a specified device. 

969  

970 Note 

971 ---- 

972 Will not initialize the GPU. 

973  

974 Parameters 

975 ---------- 

976 device_id : int, optional 

977 Device ordinal to return a :obj:`~_device.Device` object for. 

978 Default value of `None` return the currently used device. 

979  

980 """ 

981 __slots__ = ( 

982 "_device_id", 

983 "_memory_resource", 

984 "_has_inited", 

985 "_properties", 

986 "_resources", 

987 "_uuid", 

988 "_context", 

989 "__weakref__", 

990 ) 

991  

992 def __new__(cls, device_id: Device | int | None = None) -> Device:

1026 def to_system_device(self) -> 'cuda.core.system.Device': 

1027 """ 

1028 Get the corresponding :class:`cuda.core.system.Device` (which is used 

1029 for NVIDIA Management Library (NVML) access) for this 

1030 :class:`cuda.core.Device` (which is used for CUDA access). 

1031  

1032 The devices are mapped to one another by their UUID. 

1033  

1034 Returns 

1035 ------- 

1036 cuda.core.system.Device 

1037 The corresponding system-level device instance used for NVML access. 

1038 """ 

1039 from cuda.core.system._system import CUDA_BINDINGS_NVML_IS_COMPATIBLE 22z

1040  

1041 if not CUDA_BINDINGS_NVML_IS_COMPATIBLE: 22z

1042 raise RuntimeError( 

1043 "cuda.core.system.Device requires cuda-bindings 12.9.6+ for CUDA 12.x, or cuda-bindings 13.2.0+ for CUDA 13.x" 

1044 ) 

1045  

1046 from cuda.core.system import Device as SystemDevice 22z

1047 return SystemDevice(uuid=self.uuid) 22z

1060 def can_access_peer(self, peer: Device | int) -> bool: 

1061 """Check if this device can access memory from the specified peer device. 

1062  

1063 Queries whether peer-to-peer memory access is supported between this 

1064 device and the specified peer device. 

1065  

1066 Parameters 

1067 ---------- 

1068 peer : Device | int 

1069 The peer device to check accessibility to. Can be a :obj:`~_device.Device` object or device ID. 

1070 """ 

1071 peer = Device(peer) 

1072 cdef int d1 = <int> self.device_id 

1073 cdef int d2 = <int> peer.device_id 

1074 if d1 == d2: 

1075 return True 

1076 cdef int value = 0 

1077 with nogil: 

1078 HANDLE_RETURN(cydriver.cuDeviceCanAccessPeer(&value, d1, d2)) 

1079 return bool(value)

1230 def set_current(self, ctx: Context | None = None) -> Context | None: 

1231 """Set device to be used for GPU executions. 

1232  

1233 Initializes CUDA and sets the calling thread to a valid CUDA 

1234 context. By default the primary context is used, but optional `ctx` 

1235 parameter can be used to explicitly supply a :obj:`~_context.Context` object. 

1236  

1237 Providing a `ctx` causes the previous set context to be popped and returned. 

1238  

1239 Parameters 

1240 ---------- 

1241 ctx : :obj:`~_context.Context`, optional 

1242 Optional context to push onto this device's current thread stack. 

1243  

1244 Returns 

1245 ------- 

1246 :obj:`~_context.Context`, optional 

1247 Popped context. 

1248  

1249 Examples 

1250 -------- 

1251 Acts as an entry point of this object. Users always start a code by 

1252 calling this method, e.g. 

1253  

1254 >>> from cuda.core import Device 

1255 >>> dev0 = Device(0) 

1256 >>> dev0.set_current() 

1257 >>> # ... do work on device 0 ... 

1258  

1259 """

1261 cdef cydriver.CUcontext prev_ctx, curr_ctx

1363 def create_stream(self, obj: IsStreamType | None = None, options: object = None) -> Stream:
